\subsection{Detailed Description}
Header file for S\+DL video functions.

}]window should be created in high-\/\+D\+PI mode if supported \index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+T\+U\+RE@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+T\+U\+RE}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}}\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+T\+U\+RE@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+O\+U\+S\+E\+\_\+\+C\+A\+P\+T\+U\+RE}}\item[{\em

}]window has mouse captured (unrelated to I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+B\+ED) \end{description}
\end{Desc}

\item[{{\bf int}}]{x, }
\item[{{\bf int}}]{y, }
\item[{{\bf int}}]{w, }
\item[{{\bf int}}]{h, }
\item[{{\bf Uint32}}]{flags}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{_s_d_l__video_8h_a42565088bdb739a5353fd67abbe235d2}{}\label{_s_d_l__video_8h_a42565088bdb739a5353fd67abbe235d2}


Create a window with the specified position, dimensions, and flags. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em title} & The title of the window, in U\+T\+F-\/8 encoding. \\
\hline
{\em x} & The x position of the window, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a8d2f428ddef3b4ccf08915814e35d9c7}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+P\+O\+S\+\_\+\+C\+E\+N\+T\+E\+R\+ED}, or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a20917558a7e5fb159647980218726a52}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+P\+O\+S\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED}. \\
\hline
{\em y} & The y position of the window, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a8d2f428ddef3b4ccf08915814e35d9c7}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+P\+O\+S\+\_\+\+C\+E\+N\+T\+E\+R\+ED}, or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a20917558a7e5fb159647980218726a52}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+P\+O\+S\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED}. \\
\hline
{\em w} & The width of the window, in screen coordinates. \\
\hline
{\em h} & The height of the window, in screen coordinates. \\
\hline
{\em flags} & The flags for the window, a mask of any of the following\+: \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18ac7b8279bdf5e22a0b4a95aae3d846923}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+F\+U\+L\+L\+S\+C\+R\+E\+EN}, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18a5cf8af096f1870b0c2b12267cabd1f7a}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+O\+P\+E\+N\+GL}, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18adda25e98e54964c0c2ec9ac31f5e629c}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+H\+I\+D\+D\+EN}, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18af7baea7dc9c0e4f09b28793504b02e4c}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+O\+R\+D\+E\+R\+L\+E\+SS}, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18aaf59a5e2f762aa2b6d2e49b0ca220fd8}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+I\+Z\+A\+B\+LE}, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18acd8063a617f2ce05f694ecdbf56f811a}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+ED}, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18a7f08ee26b5773412a212233ddc168c5a}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+I\+M\+I\+Z\+ED}, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18aaf410e1082e45a55ef9176163610dba2}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+I\+N\+P\+U\+T\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+B\+B\+ED}, \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ab10f4fd6a082ef06fcae96860c95fb18a03ec21b04fa4e5c8cc868aa01a0c1bf3}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+D\+PI}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The id of the window created, or zero if window creation failed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
If the window is created with the S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+D\+PI flag, its size in pixels may differ from its size in screen coordinates on platforms with high-\/\+D\+PI support (e.\+g. i\+OS and Mac OS X). Use \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a5cbfffcfec91c22a7ca95fd1d5163db5}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Window\+Size()} to query the client area\textquotesingle{}s size in screen coordinates, and \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ac21851bbd91760c5bab92594a58edba3}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Drawable\+Size()} or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__render_8h_abfc0c9a50d9d1870ab7d271b7a73d8ab}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Renderer\+Output\+Size()} to query the drawable size in pixels.

\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Closest\+Display\+Mode@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Closest\+Display\+Mode}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Closest\+Display\+Mode(int display\+Index, const S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Display\+Mode $\ast$mode, S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Display\+Mode $\ast$closest)}{SDL_GetClosestDisplayMode(int displayIndex, const SDL_DisplayMode *mode, SDL_DisplayMode *closest)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf D\+E\+C\+L\+S\+P\+EC} {\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Display\+Mode}$\ast$ {\bf S\+D\+L\+C\+A\+LL} S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Closest\+Display\+Mode (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf int}}]{display\+Index, }
\item[{const {\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Display\+Mode} $\ast$}]{mode, }
\item[{{\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Display\+Mode} $\ast$}]{closest}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{_s_d_l__video_8h_a794be92ee0a9efca226fa19a635fa470}{}\label{_s_d_l__video_8h_a794be92ee0a9efca226fa19a635fa470}


Get the closest match to the requested display mode. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em display\+Index} & The index of display from which mode should be queried. \\
\hline
{\em mode} & The desired display mode \\
\hline
{\em closest} & A pointer to a display mode to be filled in with the closest match of the available display modes.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The passed in value {\ttfamily closest}, or N\+U\+LL if no matching video mode was available.
\end{DoxyReturn}
The available display modes are scanned, and {\ttfamily closest} is filled in with the closest mode matching the requested mode and returned. The mode format and refresh\+\_\+rate default to the desktop mode if they are 0. The modes are scanned with size being first priority, format being second priority, and finally checking the refresh\+\_\+rate. If all the available modes are too small, then N\+U\+LL is returned.

Get the dots/pixels-\/per-\/inch for a display. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Diagonal, horizontal and vertical D\+PI can all be optionally returned if the parameter is non-\/\+N\+U\+LL.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, or -\/1 if no D\+PI information is available or the index is out of range.
\end{DoxyReturn}

Fill in information about a specific display mode. 

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The display modes are sorted in this priority\+: \begin{DoxyItemize}
\item bits per pixel -\/$>$ more colors to fewer colors \item width -\/$>$ largest to smallest \item height -\/$>$ largest to smallest \item refresh rate -\/$>$ highest to lowest\end{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyNote}

Get the gamma ramp for a window. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em window} & The window from which the gamma ramp should be queried. \\
\hline
{\em red} & A pointer to a 256 element array of 16-\/bit quantities to hold the translation table for the red channel, or N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em green} & A pointer to a 256 element array of 16-\/bit quantities to hold the translation table for the green channel, or N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em blue} & A pointer to a 256 element array of 16-\/bit quantities to hold the translation table for the blue channel, or N\+U\+LL.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, or -\/1 if gamma ramps are unsupported.
\end{DoxyReturn}

)}\hypertarget{_s_d_l__video_8h_a5cbfffcfec91c22a7ca95fd1d5163db5}{}\label{_s_d_l__video_8h_a5cbfffcfec91c22a7ca95fd1d5163db5}


Get the size of a window\textquotesingle{}s client area. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em window} & The window to query. \\
\hline
{\em w} & Pointer to variable for storing the width, in screen coordinates. May be N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em h} & Pointer to variable for storing the height, in screen coordinates. May be N\+U\+LL.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
The window size in screen coordinates may differ from the size in pixels, if the window was created with S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+D\+PI on a platform with high-\/dpi support (e.\+g. i\+OS or OS X). Use \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ac21851bbd91760c5bab92594a58edba3}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Drawable\+Size()} or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__render_8h_abfc0c9a50d9d1870ab7d271b7a73d8ab}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Renderer\+Output\+Size()} to get the real client area size in pixels.

\hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a29b118c6932ccb94d85b5435ae1e0a19}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Size()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Get the S\+DL surface associated with the window. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The window\textquotesingle{}s framebuffer surface, or N\+U\+LL on error.
\end{DoxyReturn}
A new surface will be created with the optimal format for the window, if necessary. This surface will be freed when the window is destroyed.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
You may not combine this with 3D or the rendering A\+PI on this window.
\end{DoxyNote}

{\em window} & Window from which the drawable size should be queried \\
\hline
{\em w} & Pointer to variable for storing the width in pixels, may be N\+U\+LL \\
\hline
{\em h} & Pointer to variable for storing the height in pixels, may be N\+U\+LL\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
This may differ from \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a5cbfffcfec91c22a7ca95fd1d5163db5}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Window\+Size()} if we\textquotesingle{}re rendering to a high-\/\+D\+PI drawable, i.\+e. the window was created with S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+D\+PI on a platform with high-\/\+D\+PI support (Apple calls this \char`\"{}\+Retina\char`\"{}), and not disabled by the S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+H\+I\+N\+T\+\_\+\+V\+I\+D\+E\+O\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+D\+P\+I\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+A\+B\+L\+ED hint.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a5cbfffcfec91c22a7ca95fd1d5163db5}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Window\+Size()}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Get the swap interval for the current Open\+GL context. 

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if there is no vertical retrace synchronization, 1 if the buffer swap is synchronized with the vertical retrace, and -\/1 if late swaps happen immediately instead of waiting for the next retrace. If the system can\textquotesingle{}t determine the swap interval, or there isn\textquotesingle{}t a valid current context, this will return 0 as a safe default.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a68b0d06595d086d9244fd49afe3e8360}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Swap\+Interval()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Load\+Library@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Load\+Library}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Load\+Library@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Load\+Library}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Load\+Library(const char $\ast$path)}{SDL_GL_LoadLibrary(const char *path)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf D\+E\+C\+L\+S\+P\+EC} {\bf int} {\bf S\+D\+L\+C\+A\+LL} S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Load\+Library (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$}]{path}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{_s_d_l__video_8h_a398df9aaf43a69dc2cfaab5b306b8f91}{}\label{_s_d_l__video_8h_a398df9aaf43a69dc2cfaab5b306b8f91}


Dynamically load an Open\+GL library. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em path} & The platform dependent Open\+GL library name, or N\+U\+LL to open the default Open\+GL library.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, or -\/1 if the library couldn\textquotesingle{}t be loaded.
\end{DoxyReturn}
This should be done after initializing the video driver, but before creating any Open\+GL windows. If no Open\+GL library is loaded, the default library will be loaded upon creation of the first Open\+GL window.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If you do this, you need to retrieve all of the GL functions used in your program from the dynamic library using \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a6329bc32811639fe6f71606801cd9e7b}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Proc\+Address()}.
\end{DoxyNote}

Set the border state of a window. 

This will add or remove the window\textquotesingle{}s S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+B\+O\+R\+D\+E\+R\+L\+E\+SS flag and add or remove the border from the actual window. This is a no-\/op if the window\textquotesingle{}s border already matches the requested state.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em window} & The window of which to change the border state. \\
\hline
{\em bordered} & S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+F\+A\+L\+SE to remove border, S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+T\+R\+UE to add border.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
You can\textquotesingle{}t change the border state of a fullscreen window.
\end{DoxyNote}

\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Gamma\+Ramp@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Gamma\+Ramp}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Gamma\+Ramp@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Gamma\+Ramp}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Gamma\+Ramp(\+S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Window $\ast$window, const Uint16 $\ast$red, const Uint16 $\ast$green, const Uint16 $\ast$blue)}{SDL_SetWindowGammaRamp(SDL_Window *window, const Uint16 *red, const Uint16 *green, const Uint16 *blue)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf D\+E\+C\+L\+S\+P\+EC} {\bf int} {\bf S\+D\+L\+C\+A\+LL} S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Gamma\+Ramp (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Window} $\ast$}]{window, }
\item[{const {\bf Uint16} $\ast$}]{red, }
\item[{const {\bf Uint16} $\ast$}]{green, }
\item[{const {\bf Uint16} $\ast$}]{blue}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{_s_d_l__video_8h_a6799acf235454f519ac209ccf14caa67}{}\label{_s_d_l__video_8h_a6799acf235454f519ac209ccf14caa67}


Set the gamma ramp for a window. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em window} & The window for which the gamma ramp should be set. \\
\hline
{\em red} & The translation table for the red channel, or N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em green} & The translation table for the green channel, or N\+U\+LL. \\
\hline
{\em blue} & The translation table for the blue channel, or N\+U\+LL.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, or -\/1 if gamma ramps are unsupported.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Set the gamma translation table for the red, green, and blue channels of the video hardware. Each table is an array of 256 16-\/bit quantities, representing a mapping between the input and output for that channel. The input is the index into the array, and the output is the 16-\/bit gamma value at that index, scaled to the output color precision.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_af4d647be3bb21a33586d69d5cad87ead}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Window\+Gamma\+Ramp()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Set a window\textquotesingle{}s input grab mode.

\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Hit\+Test@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Hit\+Test}}
\index{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Hit\+Test@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Hit\+Test}!S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h@{S\+D\+L\+\_\+video.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Hit\+Test(\+S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Window $\ast$window, S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Hit\+Test callback, void $\ast$callback\+\_\+data)}{SDL_SetWindowHitTest(SDL_Window *window, SDL_HitTest callback, void *callback_data)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf D\+E\+C\+L\+S\+P\+EC} {\bf int} {\bf S\+D\+L\+C\+A\+LL} S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Hit\+Test (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Window} $\ast$}]{window, }
\item[{{\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Hit\+Test}}]{callback, }
\item[{{\bf void} $\ast$}]{callback\+\_\+data}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{_s_d_l__video_8h_a23e14e1f21f7fb3727f38fd9b0711186}{}\label{_s_d_l__video_8h_a23e14e1f21f7fb3727f38fd9b0711186}


Provide a callback that decides if a window region has special properties. 

Normally windows are dragged and resized by decorations provided by the system window manager (a title bar, borders, etc), but for some apps, it makes sense to drag them from somewhere else inside the window itself; for example, one might have a borderless window that wants to be draggable from any part, or simulate its own title bar, etc.

This function lets the app provide a callback that designates pieces of a given window as special. This callback is run during event processing if we need to tell the OS to treat a region of the window specially; the use of this callback is known as \char`\"{}hit testing.\char`\"{}

Mouse input may not be delivered to your application if it is within a special area; the OS will often apply that input to moving the window or resizing the window and not deliver it to the application.

Specifying N\+U\+LL for a callback disables hit-\/testing. Hit-\/testing is disabled by default.

Platforms that don\textquotesingle{}t support this functionality will return -\/1 unconditionally, even if you\textquotesingle{}re attempting to disable hit-\/testing.

Your callback may fire at any time, and its firing does not indicate any specific behavior (for example, on Windows, this certainly might fire when the OS is deciding whether to drag your window, but it fires for lots of other reasons, too, some unrelated to anything you probably care about {\itshape and when the mouse isn\textquotesingle{}t actually at the location it is testing}). Since this can fire at any time, you should try to keep your callback efficient, devoid of allocations, etc.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em window} & The window to set hit-\/testing on. \\
\hline
{\em callback} & The callback to call when doing a hit-\/test. \\
\hline
{\em callback\+\_\+data} & An app-\/defined void pointer passed to the callback. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on error (including unsupported). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Set the position of a window. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em window} & The window to reposition. \\
\hline
{\em x} & The x coordinate of the window in screen coordinates, or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a8d2f428ddef3b4ccf08915814e35d9c7}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+P\+O\+S\+\_\+\+C\+E\+N\+T\+E\+R\+ED} or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a20917558a7e5fb159647980218726a52}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+P\+O\+S\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED}. \\
\hline
{\em y} & The y coordinate of the window in screen coordinates, or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a8d2f428ddef3b4ccf08915814e35d9c7}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+P\+O\+S\+\_\+\+C\+E\+N\+T\+E\+R\+ED} or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a20917558a7e5fb159647980218726a52}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+P\+O\+S\+\_\+\+U\+N\+D\+E\+F\+I\+N\+ED}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The window coordinate origin is the upper left of the display.
\end{DoxyNote}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Size(\+S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Window $\ast$window, int w, int h)}{SDL_SetWindowSize(SDL_Window *window, int w, int h)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf D\+E\+C\+L\+S\+P\+EC} {\bf void} {\bf S\+D\+L\+C\+A\+LL} S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Set\+Window\+Size (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Window} $\ast$}]{window, }
\item[{{\bf int}}]{w, }
\item[{{\bf int}}]{h}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{_s_d_l__video_8h_a29b118c6932ccb94d85b5435ae1e0a19}{}\label{_s_d_l__video_8h_a29b118c6932ccb94d85b5435ae1e0a19}


Set the size of a window\textquotesingle{}s client area. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em window} & The window to resize. \\
\hline
{\em w} & The width of the window, in screen coordinates. Must be $>$0. \\
\hline
{\em h} & The height of the window, in screen coordinates. Must be $>$0.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
You can\textquotesingle{}t change the size of a fullscreen window, it automatically matches the size of the display mode.
\end{DoxyNote}
The window size in screen coordinates may differ from the size in pixels, if the window was created with S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+A\+L\+L\+O\+W\+\_\+\+H\+I\+G\+H\+D\+PI on a platform with high-\/dpi support (e.\+g. i\+OS or OS X). Use \hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_ac21851bbd91760c5bab92594a58edba3}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+G\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Drawable\+Size()} or \hyperlink{_s_d_l__render_8h_abfc0c9a50d9d1870ab7d271b7a73d8ab}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Renderer\+Output\+Size()} to get the real client area size in pixels.

\hyperlink{_s_d_l__video_8h_a5cbfffcfec91c22a7ca95fd1d5163db5}{S\+D\+L\+\_\+\+Get\+Window\+Size()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Initialize the video subsystem, optionally specifying a video driver. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em driver\+\_\+name} & Initialize a specific driver by name, or N\+U\+LL for the default video driver.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, -\/1 on error
\end{DoxyReturn}
This function initializes the video subsystem; setting up a connection to the window manager, etc, and determines the available display modes and pixel formats, but does not initialize a window or graphics mode.
